The sudden burst of violence sends a wave of shock through the Copper Cup. Mara, the barkeep, slams a hand down on the counter, her eyes wide as she shouts for everyone to stay back. Brin lunges toward the back door, shouting a warning to the other patrons. Edda pulls a chair from under her table and hurls it toward the commotion, while Lysa scrambles to the bar, her face pale. Thom, already half-raised from his seat, drops his mug, the liquid spilling across the floor as he draws his own weapon, eyes fixed on you. The lanterns sway, casting flickering shadows over the chaos. Shouts, curses, and the clatter of chairs fill the air as the tavern erupts into a frenzy, the patrons scrambling for cover or to intervene. Mitch, bleeding but still standing, glares at you through his pain, his grip on his belt loosening as he tries to steady himself.
